<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a> (11854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бровь.html>бровя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">povesti brovjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to raise one's brows; lift one's eyebrows</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плечо́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povodítʹ</b> plečóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move one's shoulder</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бровь.html>бро́вью</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повести.html>повёл</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on i bróvʹju/úxom ne povjól</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> he did not turn a hair; he did not bat an eyelid</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk, to take around
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́трам</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:выставка.html>вы́ставкам</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povodítʹ</b> kovó-libo po teátram (výstavkam)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take smb to theatres (exhibitions)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povodítʹ</b> lóšadʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to walk a horse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for a while</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">daj mne <b>povodítʹ</b> mašínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">let me drive (the car) for a while</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povodíl</b> i xvátit!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you've driven the car enough!; you've had your bit of driving!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поворачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поворачивать.html>повора́чивать</a> (4169)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">повороти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поворачивать.html>повора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">повороти́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn, to swing</li>
<li>to turn <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to change direction of one's motion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">повороти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are both possible perfectives of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поворачивать.html>повора́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povoráčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but the latter is specifically low-colloquial, while the former is normal register or colloquial.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поворачиваться.html>повора́чиваться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povoráčivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повернуться.html>поверну́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povernútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">повороти́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povorotítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повредить.html>повреди́ть</a> (5345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вредить.html>вреди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vredítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повредить.html>повреди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povredítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вредить.html>вреди́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поврежда́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to injure, to harm, to hurt, to damage, to cause damage</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повреждение.html>поврежде́ние</a> (6459)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повреждение.html>поврежде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povreždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повреждение.html>поврежде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повреждение.html>поврежде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повреждение.html>поврежде́ний</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повстречаться.html>повстреча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povstrečátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to meet, to run into <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental or + dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повстречать.html>повстреча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povstrečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́р</a> (24202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povtór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>repetition, repeat, rebroadcast, rerun
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изобиловать.html>изоби́лует</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́рами</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rečʹ izobílujet <b>povtórami</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the speech is highly repetitious/repetitive</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:функция.html>фу́нкция</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́ра</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">fúnkcija <b>povtóra</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">repeat function</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автоматический.html>автомати́ческий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повтор.html>повто́р</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:набор.html>набо́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>номера</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">avtomatíčeskij <b>povtór</b> nabóra nomera</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">automatic redial</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
